<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; line-height: 20pt; text-align: left"><!--page language="java" pageEncoding="UTF-8--><strong><span lang="EN-US"><font size="3">Model designation:</font></span></strong></p>
<h3 style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; text-align: center"><span lang="EN-US"><img height="198" alt="" width="700" border="0" src="/products/image/Cable%20drum/long-timely%20hindered%20rotation%20torque%20motor%20type%20cable%20drum/1.gif" /></span></h3>
<p class="MsoHeading9" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; text-align: center">&nbsp;</p>
<p class="MsoHeading9" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; text-align: left"><span lang="EN-US"><strong><em><font size="5">Guide for model selection</font></em></strong></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; text-align: left"><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; line-height: 20pt; text-align: left"><span style="font-family: 宋体">●</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt"> The installation height of the cable drum</span><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 宋体">&le;</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt">3m.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; line-height: 20pt; text-align: left"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Based on the specification (overall dimension, cable core number for power, cable capacity length, the voltage,) selected the cable drum which are required from various table.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; line-height: 20pt; text-align: left"><span style="font-family: 宋体">●</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt"> The installation height of the cable drum</span><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 宋体">＞</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt">3m.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; line-height: 20pt; text-align: left"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt">1.Counting the torque which the cable drum is needed based on the formula T=h.d.w.1/J<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; line-height: 20pt; text-align: left"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt">Note: The output torque of the cable drum must be great than torque counted.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; line-height: 20pt; text-align: left"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>T:<span>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>torque<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; line-height: 20pt; text-align: left"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>H:<span>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>installation height of cable drum<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; line-height: 20pt; text-align: left"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>D1:<span>&nbsp; </span>coil bar diameter of the cable drum<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; line-height: 20pt; text-align: left"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>W:<span>&nbsp; </span><span>&nbsp;</span>length unit of the cable<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; line-height: 20pt; text-align: left"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span>J :<span>&nbsp; </span><span>&nbsp;</span>capacity is 0.85<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; line-height: 20pt; text-align: left"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt">2.Based on torque counted, cable specification (cable core number for power, cable core number for control, voltage, and the model designation), thus , confirmed<span>&nbsp; </span>the cable drum model.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; line-height: 20pt; text-align: left"><span style="font-family: 宋体">●</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt"> Special purposes of products can be noted the requirements as cable data, cable capacity length, voltage, cart operating speed and installation height of the cable drum should be specified when ordered, so we can<span>&nbsp; </span>assist customer<span>&nbsp; </span>to confirm the cable model.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; line-height: 20pt; text-align: left"><span style="font-family: 宋体">●</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt"> Pattern selection attention:<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; line-height: 20pt; text-align: left"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt">1.Coiling up in single row, the value W of coil bar width confirmation: round cable width<span>&nbsp; </span>is l.1 times of the diameter, flat cable width is1.2 times<span>&nbsp; </span>of<span>&nbsp; </span>cable' s.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoBodyText" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; line-height: 20pt; text-align: left"><span lang="EN-US">2.Cable drum for control, increasing one phrase, and<span>&nbsp; </span>the total length should<span>&nbsp; </span>rise 25 mm<span>&nbsp; </span>accordingly.</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; text-align: left"><b><span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; line-height: 20pt; text-align: left"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt">Features:</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; text-indent: 26.25pt; line-height: 20pt; text-align: left"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt">JM </span><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 宋体">□</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt">D series is<span>&nbsp; </span>a kind of long-timely hindered rotation torque motor type cable drum. Which is widely used in large scale mechanical equipment that need to horizontal move such as the material fetching machine, door pedestal crane, loading ship machine, the container hoist, tower crane, etc. Power source and signal source lie in middle or ends of distance. It transmits power source and control signal through cable drum to be coiling up and spooling off cable.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; text-indent: 26.25pt; line-height: 20pt; text-align: left"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt">&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; line-height: 20pt; text-align: left"><b><i><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 14pt">Long-timely hindered rotation torque motor type cable drum structure:<o:p></o:p></span></i></b></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; line-height: 20pt; text-align: left">&nbsp;</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; line-height: 20pt; text-align: left"><span style="font-family: 宋体">●</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt"> <strong>Main machine</strong>:<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; line-height: 20pt; text-align: left"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt">1</span><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 宋体">、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt">Power force part:<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; line-height: 20pt; text-align: left"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'Times New Roman'">Long-term<span>&nbsp; </span>hindered rotation<span>&nbsp; </span>torque motor (take the brake), special-purpose reductor<span>&nbsp; </span>machine, collector slip ring group .</span></p>
<p style="text-align: center"><img height="314" alt="" width="700" border="0" src="/products/image/Cable%20drum/long-timely%20hindered%20rotation%20torque%20motor%20type%20cable%20drum/2.gif" /><br />
&nbsp;</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; line-height: 20pt; text-align: left"><span style="font-size: 12px"><span lang="EN-US">1. fixed bolt<span>&nbsp; </span>2. motor axles<span>&nbsp; </span>3. motor outer covers<span>&nbsp; </span>4. making plate<span>&nbsp; </span>5. brake block 6. presses plate<span>&nbsp; </span>7. brake spring<span>&nbsp; </span>8. excitation coils<span>&nbsp; </span>9. manual bolts 10. electro-magnets of shells<span>&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>11. a pull rod of press<span>&nbsp; </span>12. manual regulating ring<span>&nbsp; </span>13. manual regulating ring<span>&nbsp; </span>14. regulating spring.</span></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; line-height: 20pt; text-align: left"><span style="font-family: 宋体">●</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt"> <strong>Cable capacity part<o:p></o:p></strong></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; text-indent: 21.75pt; line-height: 20pt; text-align: left"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt">Spool: can be divided into many row and single row twined, To facilitate transporting, spool of diameter </span><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 宋体">&le;</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt"> 2.4m is whole structure; </span><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 宋体">＞</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt">2.4m are parts, assembling on- site. <span>&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; line-height: 20pt; text-align: center"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt">&nbsp;<img height="681" alt="" width="550" border="0" src="/products/image/Cable%20drum/long-timely%20hindered%20rotation%20torque%20motor%20type%20cable%20drum/4.gif" /></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; line-height: 20pt; text-align: center"><br />
&nbsp;</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; line-height: 20pt; text-align: left"><span style="font-family: 宋体">●</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt"><strong> cable erum electric principle diagram</strong></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; line-height: 20pt; text-align: center"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt"><strong><o:p><img height="303" alt="" width="800" border="0" src="/products/image/Cable%20drum/long-timely%20hindered%20rotation%20torque%20motor%20type%20cable%20drum/5.gif" /></o:p></strong></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; line-height: 20pt; text-align: center"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt">&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; line-height: 20pt; text-align: left"><span style="font-family: 宋体">●</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt"><strong> Cable drum operation principle:<o:p></o:p></strong></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; line-height: 20pt; text-align: left"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Long-timely hindered rotation type which the power part of cable drum and regulating speed part beared by motor with uniqueness electrical and mechanical, which has a wide of speed adjustment and softer mechanical characteristics. The corresponding change of the rotational speed of the motor happens when changing in load, namely load increases the rotational speed to drop, load drops the rotational speed raises. It features all long and steady operation at whatever of their torque and rotational speed of mechanical curves.<span>&nbsp; </span>So can guarantee the cable obtain proper coiling speed and pulling force on the corresponding radius.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; line-height: 20pt; text-align: left"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt">1. Coiling up: Cable motor outputs torque as power force, coiling up cable by reductor running the spool to coil up cable.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; line-height: 20pt; text-align: left"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt">2. Release cable: Motor leaves strength of hindering from torque, preventing the cable from drawing spool fast, it guarantees putting synchronous of releasing cable.<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; line-height: 20pt; text-align: left"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt">3. When machinery shutting down, long- timely motor have plate type often close brake, which can guarantee the cable will not back fall from a plate for the action of the gravity<span>&nbsp; </span>when<span>&nbsp; </span>power cutting off. </span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; line-height: 20pt; text-align: left">&nbsp;</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; line-height: 20pt; text-align: center"><span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: -0.5pt">JM10D-</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; letter-spacing: -0.5pt">□</span><span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: -0.5pt">4P JM10D-</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; letter-spacing: -0.5pt">□</span><span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: -0.5pt">19K</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; letter-spacing: -0.5pt">～</span><span lang="EN-US" style="letter-spacing: -0.5pt">24K </span></p>

</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; line-height: 20pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt">Long-timely hindered rotation torque motor type cable drum electrical data and features:<o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; line-height: 20pt"><span style="font-size: 13px"><span lang="EN-US">1.1 The cable is invariable to tension among the full coil bar from empty one, applied to under the working situation of long-timely low-speed, frequent operating in positive and oppose rotation.</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; line-height: 20pt"><span style="font-size: 13px"><span lang="EN-US">1.2 Different from general motor is that it supplied with small current and it can long -timely hindered rotate,<span>&nbsp; </span>reverse rotate.</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; line-height: 20pt"><span style="font-family: Arial"><span style="font-size: 13px"><span lang="EN-US">1.3 It has tested in 8-10 hours hindered rotation before assembling, the motor rises warmly &lt; 65K in hot state, hindered rotation torque decreases in 5% of the ranges.<span>&nbsp; </span></span></span></span><span style="font-family: Arial">&nbsp;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; line-height: 20pt"><span style="font-family: Arial"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>Brake consists<span>&nbsp; </span>of<span>&nbsp; </span>magnetism<span>&nbsp; </span>yoke, excitation coil, spring, brake disc, armature, gear wheel cover, manual releasing the device, screw etc. </span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; line-height: 20pt"><span style="font-family: Arial"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt"><span>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span>The brake is installed and covered in the back of the motor, adjusting and installing screw reach suitable air (space) crack value, and brake disc and gear wheel cover<span>&nbsp; </span>band motor drive shaft.</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; text-indent: 21.75pt; line-height: 20pt"><span style="font-family: Arial"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt">When excitation coil of brake being at putting through the rated voltage, the electric magnetic force sucks the armature, making armature be independent from brake disc (release). The axle of the motor drives brake disc being under normal operation, when the motor cuts out, and the brake cuts out at the same time too, the spring oppressing the armature at this moment which forcing between brake disc and armature and ring flange produce the torque of friction, making the axle of the motor park to rotate fast.</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; text-indent: 21.75pt; line-height: 20pt"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt"><o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; line-height: 20pt"><span style="font-family: Arial"><strong><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt">2</span><span style="font-size: 12pt">、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt">Electricity (the signal) transmitting part<span>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span></span></strong></span><strong><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt"><o:p></o:p></span></strong></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0cm 0cm 0pt; text-indent: 21.75pt; line-height: 20pt"><span style="font-family: Arial"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt">Collector ring chamber can be divided into power and signal transmission from usage, and can be divided into 380V</span><span style="font-size: 12pt">、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt">500V</span><span style="font-size: 12pt">、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt">3KV</span><span style="font-size: 12pt">、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt">6KV</span><span style="font-size: 12pt">、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt">10KV, etc. according to the grade of voltage.</span></span></p>
